Note that number and size of\n73:      * the produced records should be relatively small. Serialization Interfaces\\n\\nIn the Apache Kafka repository (`github.com/sg-evals/kafka--0753c489`), the fundamental serialization interfaces are defined under `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/serialization/`:\\n\\n1. **Serializer Interface** (`Serializer.java`): \\n   - Converts objects to bytes using `serialize(String topic, T data)` method\\n   - Supports configuration via `configure(Map<String, ?> configs, boolean isKey)`\\n   - Extends `Closeable` for resource management\\n   - Can optionally implement additional interfaces like `ClusterResourceListener` and `Monitorable`\\n\\n2. **Deserializer Interface** (`Deserializer.java`):\\n   - Converts bytes to objects using `deserialize(String topic, byte[] data)` method\\n   - Also supports deserializing from `ByteBuffer` via `deserialize(String topic, Headers headers, ByteBuffer data)`\\n   - Extends `Closeable` for resource management\\n   - Can be combined with `ClusterResourceListener` for metadata access\\n\\n### Flink Deserialization Schema\\n\\nIn the Apache Flink repository (`github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc`), Flink defines its own deserialization abstraction:\\n\\n**DeserializationSchema Interface** (`flink-core/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/api/common/serialization/DeserializationSchema.java`):\\n- Converts byte messages into Flink data types (Java/Scala objects)\\n- Provides methods:\\n  - `deserialize(byte[] message)` - deserialize a single message\\n  - `deserialize(byte[] message, Collector<T> out)` - output multiple records via Collector\\n  - `isEndOfStream(T nextElement)` - signal end of stream\\n  - `open(InitializationContext context)` - initialization with metrics and class loader access\\n- Extends both `Serializable` and `ResultTypeQueryable<T>`\\n- Designed for use with various data sources including Apache Kafka\\n\\n### Connection Point\\n\\nThe serialization boundary is bridged through the Kafka connector module (`flink-connector-kafka`), which is an external dependency to the core Flink repository. The connector would typically contain:\\n\\n- **KafkaDeserializationSchema** (mentioned in Flink 1.8+ release notes) - gives direct access to Kafka's `ConsumerRecord`\\n- Adapter implementations that wrap Kafka's `Deserializer` interface to implement Flink's `DeserializationSchema`\\n- Classes like `KafkaRecordDeserializationSchema` that handle the conversion between Kafka's Deserializer and Flink's DeserializationSchema\\n\\nNote: The `flink-connector-kafka` module was not found in the provided Flink repository snapshot as it is maintained as an external module. The core Flink repository references it as a dependency in pom.xml files (version 3.0.0-1.17 in the provided snapshot).\\n\\n### Key Design Differences\\n\\n- **Kafka's Deserializer**: Topic-aware, receives `(topic, byte[], headers)` tuple, returns a single typed object\\n- **Flink's DeserializationSchema**: More feature-rich, supports:\\n  - Multiple records output per message via Collector\\n  - Lifecycle management through `InitializationContext`\\n  - Type information for Flink's type system via `ResultTypeQueryable`\\n  - End-of-stream signal detection\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1824,"cache_read_input_tokens":98040,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1824},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"73fee9c3-9a62-4235-84bf-aa41f12f4e4c","uuid":"84b05eef-fc1c-4157-bb20-aaba41295a7d"}

`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/serialization/`:\\n\\n1. **Serializer Interface** (`Serializer.java`): \\n   - Converts objects to bytes using `serialize(String topic, T data)`
